import Client\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\nROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]\nREPORTS = ROOT / \"reports\"\nBEST = REPORTS / \"best_sweep.csv\"\n\ndef env_or_fail(key):\n    v =   load_dotenv()\n    token = env_or_fail(\"NOTION_TOKEN\")\n    db_id = env_or_fail(\"NOTION_DB_ID\")\n    notion = Client(auth=token)\n\n    if not BEST.exists():\n        print(f\"best_sweep.csv ì—†ìŒ: {BEST}\")\n        return\n\n    with BEST.open(encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n        for row in reader:\n            # ê¸°ëŒ€ ì»¬ëŸ¼: strategy, fast, slow, = int(float(row.get(\"fast\", 0)))\n            slow = int(float(row.get(\"slow\", 0)))\n            fee = to_number(row.get(\"fee\"))\n            final_equity =             \"Date\": {\"date\": {\"start\": date_str}},\n              \"StrategyName\": {\"title\": [{\"text\": {\"content\": strategy}}]},\n              \"Fast\": {\"number\": fast},\n
